default swaps. \n * The protection buyer periodically pays fixed coupons to the protection seller until the expiry, \n * and in return, the protection buyer receives the bond of a defaulted constituent legal entity for par.  \n */\n@BeanDefinition\npublic final class CdsIndex\n    implements Product, Resolvable<ResolvedCdsIndex>, ImmutableBean, Serializable {\n\n  /**\n   * Whether the CDS index is buy or sell.\n   * <p>\n   * A value of 'Buy' implies buying protection, where the fixed coupon is paid\n   * and the protection is received  in the event of default.\n   * A value of @PropertyDefinition(validate = \"notNull\")\n  private final DaysAdjustment stepinDateOffset;\n  /**\n   * The number of days between valuation date and settlement date.\n   * <p>\n   * It is usually @PropertyDefinition(validate = \"notNull\")\n  private final DaysAdjustment settlementDateOffset;\n\n  //-------------------------------------------------------------------------\n  /**\n   * Creates double fixedRate) {\n\n    PeriodicSchedule accrualSchedule = PeriodicSchedule.builder()\n        .businessDayAdjustment(BusinessDayAdjustment.of(BusinessDayConventions.FOLLOWING, calendar))\n        .startDate(startDate)\n        .endDate(endDate)\n        .startDateBusinessDayAdjustment(BusinessDayAdjustment.NONE)\n        .endDateBusinessDayAdjustment(BusinessDayAdjustment.NONE)\n        .frequency(paymentFrequency)\n        .rollConvention(RollConventions.NONE)\n        .stubConvention(StubConvention.SMART_INITIAL)\n        .build();\n    return new CdsIndex(\n        buySell,\n        cdsIndexId,\n        legalEntityIds,\n        currency,\n        notional,\n        accrualSchedule,\n        fixedRate,\n        DayCounts.ACT_360,\n        PaymentOnDefault.ACCRUED_PREMIUM,\n .yearFraction(modifiedPeriod.yearFraction(dayCount, adjustedSchedule))\n        .build());\n    ImmutableList<CreditCouponPaymentPeriod> paymentPeriods = accrualPeriods.build();\n\n    return CreditRatesMarketDataLookup} must be specified.\n * The supported built-in measures are:\n * <ul>\n *   <li>{@linkplain Measures#PRESENT_VALUE Present value}\n *   <li>{@linkplain Measures#RESOLVED_TARGET Resolved trade}\n * </ul>\n * <p>\n * The \"natural\" currency is the currency of the underlying CDS index, which is limited to be single-currency.\n */\npublic class CdsTrancheTradeCalculationFunction\n    implements CalculationFunction<CdsTrancheTrade> {\n\n  /**\n   * The calculations by measure.\n   */\n  private static final ImmutableMap<Measure, SingleMeasureCalculation> CALCULATORS =\n      ImmutableMap.<Measure, SingleMeasureCalculation>builder()\n          .put(Measures.PRESENT_VALUE, CdsTrancheCalculations.DEFAULT::presentValue)\n          .put(Measures.RESOLVED_TARGET, (rt, smd, rd) -> rt)\n          .build();\n\n  private static final ImmutableSet<Measure> MEASURES = CALCULATORS.keySet();\n\n  /**\n   * Creates an instance.\n   */\n {\n    return target.getInfo().getId().map(id -> id.toString());\n  }\n\n  @Override\n  public Currency naturalCurrency(CdsTrancheTrade trade, ReferenceData refData) {\n    return trade.getProduct().getUnderlyingIndex().getCurrency();\n  }\n\n  //-------------------------------------------------------------------------\n  @Override\n  public FunctionRequirements requirements(\n trade.getProduct();\n    StandardId cdsIndexId = product.getUnderlyingIndex().getCdsIndexId();\n    Currency currency = product.getUnderlyingIndex().getCurrency();\n\n    // use lookup to build requirements\n    CreditRatesMarketDataLookup lookup = parameters.getParameter(CreditRatesMarketDataLookup.class);\n    return lookup.requirements(cdsIndexId, currency);\n  }\n\n  //-------------------------------------------------------------------------\n  @Override\n  public Map<Measure, Result<?>> calculate(\n      CdsTrancheTrade trade,\n      Set<Measure> measures,\n      CalculationParameters parameters,\n      ScenarioMarketData scenarioMarketData,\n      ReferenceData refData) {\n\n    // resolve the trade once for all measures and all scenarios\n    ResolvedCdsTrancheTrade resolved = trade.resolve(refData);\n\n    // use lookup to query market data\n    CreditRatesMarketDataLookup ledLookup = parameters.getParameter(CreditRatesMarketDataLookup.class);\n    CreditRatesScenarioMarketData marketData = ledLookup.marketDataView(scenarioMarketData);\n\n    // loop around measures, calculating all scenarios for one measure\n    Map<Measure, Result<?>> results = new HashMap<>();\n    for (Measure measure : measures) {\n      results.put(measure, calculate(measure, resolved, marketData, refData));\n    }\n    return results;\n  }\n\n  // calculate one measure\n  private Result<?> calculate(\n      Measure measure,\n      ResolvedCdsTrancheTrade trade,\n      CreditRatesScenarioMarketData marketData,\n      ReferenceData refData) {\n\n    SingleMeasureCalculation calculator = CALCULATORS.get(measure);\n    if (calculator == null) {\n      return Result.failure(FailureReason.UNSUPPORTED, \"Unsupported measure for CdsTrancheTrade: {}\", measure);\n    }\n    return Result.of(() -> calculator.calculate(trade, marketData, refData));\n  }\n\n Integration Points\n   ├── CreditRatesMarketDataLookup (fetches market data)\n   ├── CalculationFunction registration (via classpath scanning)\n   └── Measures framework (standard Strata measures)\n```\n\n## Key Design Decisions\n\n### 1. Product Structure\n- **Composition over Inheritance**: CdsTranche wraps CdsIndex rather than extending it. This allows:\n  - Clean separation of concerns\n  - Flexibility to change index definition without affecting tranche\n  - Reuse of CdsIndex validation and payment schedule logic\n\n### 2. Tranche Representation\n- **Standardized Boundaries**: Attachment and detachment points as doubles (0.0-1.0)\n  - Allows standard CDO tranche notation (e.g., 3-6% tranche)\n  - Matches market conventions for synthetic CDOs\n  - Simple to validate and compare\n\n### 3. Pricing Architecture\n- **Delegation Pattern**: IsdaCdsTranchePricer composes existing pricers\n  - Minimizes code duplication\n  - Leverages battle-tested ISDA model implementations\n  - Future enhancements can improve loss distribution calculations\n\n### 4. Calculation Integration\n- **Standard Framework**: Uses existing Strata measure and market data infrastructure\n  - Consistent with CDS/CdsIndex patterns\n  - Automatic scenario support\n  - Easy extension for additional measures (CS01, IR01, etc.)\n\n## Code Quality Patterns Applied\n\n### Joda-Beans Compliance\n- All classes marked with `@BeanDefinition`\n- Proper property validation via `@PropertyDefinition` annotations\n- Explicit Meta and Builder classes with correct signatures\n- Return type `Class<? extends T>` for beanType() methods (not `Class<?>`)\n- All @Override annotations present\n- Proper serialVersionUID fields\n- Complete equals/hashCode/toString methods\n\n### Immutability\n- All product/trade classes implement `ImmutableBean`\n- Fields are final (enforced by Joda-Beans)\n- No setters on resolved classes\n- Builders for construction\n\n### Error Handling\n- `ArgChecker` validation for tranche boundaries in resolve()\n- `JodaBeanUtils.notNull()` for non-null assertions\n- Range validation: `0.0 ≤ attachmentPoint < detachmentPoint ≤ 1.0`\n- FailureReason.UNSUPPORTED for unimplemented measures\n\n### Extensibility\n- Additional measures can be added to CdsTrancheTradeCalculationFunction.CALCULATORS map\n- Pricing logic can be enhanced in IsdaCdsTranchePricer.presentValueInternal()\n- Sensitivity calculations (priceSensitivity) are defined but can be enhanced\n\n## Compilation Status\n\nAll files successfully compile with:\n- ✅ Maven checkstyle validation (no formatting issues)\n- ✅ Java syntax validation (proper Joda-Bean structure)\n- ✅ Type safety (proper generic type signatures)\n- ✅ No breaking changes to existing code\n\nModules confirmed compiled:\n- modules/product/src/main/java/... Pricer Layer\n   └── IsdaCdsTranchePricer (prices ResolvedCdsTrancheTrade)\n       └── Computes PV using tranche boundaries\n\n3. Calculation/Measure Layer\n   ├── CdsTrancheTradeCalculationFunction (entry point)\n   ├── Delegates to CdsTrancheCalculations\n   └── CdsTrancheCalculations invokes IsdaCdsTranchePricer\n\n4. Integration Points\n   ├── CreditRatesMarketDataLookup (fetches market data)\n   ├── CalculationFunction registration (via classpath scanning)\n   └── Measures framework (standard Strata measures)\n```\n\n## Key Design Decisions\n\n### 1. Product Structure\n- **Composition over Inheritance**: CdsTranche wraps CdsIndex rather than extending it. This allows:\n  - Clean separation of concerns\n  - Flexibility to change index definition without affecting tranche\n  - Reuse of CdsIndex validation and payment schedule logic\n\n### 2. Tranche Representation\n- **Standardized Boundaries**: Attachment and detachment points as doubles (0.0-1.0)\n  - Allows standard CDO tranche notation (e.g., 3-6% tranche)\n  - Matches market conventions for synthetic CDOs\n  - Simple to validate and compare\n\n### 3. Pricing Architecture\n- **Delegation Pattern**: IsdaCdsTranchePricer composes existing pricers\n  - Minimizes code duplication\n  - Leverages battle-tested ISDA model implementations\n  - Future enhancements can improve loss distribution calculations\n\n### 4. Calculation Integration\n- **Standard Framework**: Uses existing Strata measure and market data infrastructure\n  - Consistent with CDS/CdsIndex patterns\n  - Automatic scenario support\n  - Easy extension for additional measures (CS01, IR01, etc.)\n\n## Code Quality Patterns Applied\n\n### Joda-Beans Compliance\n- All classes marked with `@BeanDefinition`\n- Proper property validation via `@PropertyDefinition` annotations\n- Explicit Meta and Builder classes with correct signatures\n- Return type `Class<? extends T>` for beanType() methods (not `Class<?>`)\n- All @Override annotations present\n- Proper serialVersionUID fields\n- Complete equals/hashCode/toString methods\n\n### Immutability\n- All product/trade classes implement `ImmutableBean`\n- Fields are final (enforced by Joda-Beans)\n- No setters on resolved classes\n- Builders for construction\n\n### Error Handling\n- `ArgChecker` validation for tranche boundaries in resolve()\n- `JodaBeanUtils.notNull()` for non-null assertions\n- Range validation: `0.0 ≤ attachmentPoint < detachmentPoint ≤ 1.0`\n- FailureReason.UNSUPPORTED for unimplemented measures\n\n### Extensibility\n- Additional measures can be added to CdsTrancheTradeCalculationFunction.CALCULATORS map\n- Pricing logic can be enhanced in IsdaCdsTranchePricer.presentValueInternal()\n- Sensitivity calculations (priceSensitivity) are defined but can be enhanced\n\n## Compilation Status\n\nAll files successfully compile with:\n- ✅ Maven checkstyle validation (no formatting issues)\n- ✅ Java syntax validation (proper Joda-Bean structure)\n- ✅ Type safety (proper generic type signatures)\n- ✅ No breaking changes to existing code\n\nModules confirmed compiled:\n- modules/product/src/main/java/...
